--criar tabela FASES_EDICAO

-- Table: public."Fases_Edicao"

-- DROP TABLE public."Fases_Edicao";

CREATE TABLE public."Fases_Edicao"
(
  codigo integer NOT NULL,
  "Descricao" character varying,
  CONSTRAINT "Fases_Edicao_pkey" PRIMARY KEY (codigo)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);
ALTER TABLE public."Fases_Edicao"
  OWNER TO postgres;
COMMENT ON TABLE public."Fases_Edicao"
  IS 'Descrição das fases da Edição de uma Carta Topográfica';



--tabela edicao - mudança de valores dos status (modificar mapa de valores qgis e categorização )

UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_1' WHERE status = '0';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_2' WHERE status = '11';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_3' WHERE status = '1';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_4' WHERE status = '2';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_5' WHERE status = '3';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_6' WHERE status = '5';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_7' WHERE status = '9';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_8' WHERE status = '7';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '_9' WHERE status = '10';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '1' WHERE status = '_1';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '2' WHERE status = '_2';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '3' WHERE status = '_3';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '4' WHERE status = '_4';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '5' WHERE status = '_5';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '6' WHERE status = '_6';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '7' WHERE status = '_7';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '8' WHERE status = '_8';
UPDATE "public"."edicao" SET status = '9' WHERE status = '_9';



--tabela edicao - mudança de colunas (modificar mapa de valores, rotulo e categorização  no qgis)

ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" RENAME COLUMN operador TO editor;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" RENAME COLUMN inicio TO inicioedicao;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" RENAME COLUMN termino TO terminoedicao;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" RENAME COLUMN revisor TO revisor1;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" RENAME COLUMN inic TO inicio1rev;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" RENAME COLUMN term TO termino1rev;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" ADD COLUMN revisor2 character varying;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" ADD COLUMN inicio2rev character varying;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao" ADD COLUMN termino2rev character varying;



-- Table: public.usuarios

-- DROP TABLE public.usuarios;

CREATE TABLE public.usuarios
(
    codigo integer NOT NULL,
    nome character varying COLLATE pg_catalog."default",
    funcao integer,
    login character varying COLLATE pg_catalog."default",
    senha character varying COLLATE pg_catalog."default",
    CONSTRAINT usuarios_pkey PRIMARY KEY (codigo)
)
WITH (
    OIDS = FALSE
)
TABLESPACE pg_default;

ALTER TABLE public.usuarios
    OWNER to postgres;
COMMENT ON TABLE public.usuarios
    IS 'Lista dos usuarios que trabalham no projeto';

-- cria tabela funcoes e insere os valores

CREATE TABLE public."funcoes"
(
  codigo integer NOT NULL,
  nome character varying,
  descricao character varying,
  CONSTRAINT "funcoes_pkey" PRIMARY KEY (codigo)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);
ALTER TABLE public."funcoes"
  OWNER TO postgres;
COMMENT ON TABLE public."funcoes"
  IS 'Lista funcoes dos usuarios no projeto';

--alterar forekey tabela edicao -- antes precisa mudar o tipo dos usuarios para integer

ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao"
  ADD FOREIGN KEY (editor) REFERENCES "public"."usuarios" (codigo) ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao"
  ADD FOREIGN KEY (revisor1) REFERENCES "public"."usuarios" (codigo) ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao"
  ADD FOREIGN KEY (revisor2) REFERENCES "public"."usuarios" (codigo) ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION;
ALTER TABLE "public"."edicao"
  ADD FOREIGN KEY (status) REFERENCES public."Fases_Edicao" (codigo) ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION;

-- ja foi criado no localhost e no 22 ( banco de ligacoes_mi)

-- Table: public.ligacao_mi

-- DROP TABLE public.ligacao_mi;

CREATE TABLE public.ligacao_mi
(
  geom geometry(Polygon,4674),
  mi character varying NOT NULL,
  o character varying,
  s character varying,
  se character varying,
  so character varying,
  l character varying,
  n character varying,
  no character varying,
  ne character varying,
  CONSTRAINT ligacao_mi_pkey PRIMARY KEY (mi)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);
ALTER TABLE public.ligacao_mi
  OWNER TO postgres;

-- Index: public.sidx_ligacao_mi_geom

-- DROP INDEX public.sidx_ligacao_mi_geom;

CREATE INDEX sidx_ligacao_mi_geom
  ON public.ligacao_mi
  USING gist
  (geom);

--criar tabela Situacao e criar coluna situacao, integer na tabela usuarios

CREATE TABLE public.situacao
(
    codigo integer NOT NULL,
    descricao character varying,
    PRIMARY KEY (codigo)
)
WITH (
    OIDS = FALSE
);

ALTER TABLE public.situacao
    OWNER to postgres;
COMMENT ON TABLE public.situacao
    IS 'Situação do status de trabalho, onde o militar esta trabalhando';

INSERT INTO public.situacao (codigo, descricao) VALUES (1, 'Pronto');

ALTER TABLE public.usuarios
    ADD COLUMN situacao integer;

CREATE TABLE public.postos_graduacoes
(
    codigo integer NOT NULL,
    nome character varying COLLATE pg_catalog."default",
    grupos character varying COLLATE pg_catalog."default",
    abrev character varying COLLATE pg_catalog."default",
    CONSTRAINT postos_graduacoes_pkey PRIMARY KEY (codigo)
)
WITH (
    OIDS = FALSE
)
TABLESPACE pg_default;

ALTER TABLE public.postos_graduacoes
    OWNER to postgres;
